<p>Unknown. The only cognate found <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy">waarje</i>.

***warenhuis.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuis</a> (10295)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waren.html>waren</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">goods</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:huis.html>huis</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">house</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, calque of  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Warenhaus</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuis</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuizen.html>warenhuizen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuisje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A department store.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl">warenmagazijn</span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A warehouse.
<dl><dd><span class="nyms synonym"><span class="defdate">Synonym:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pakhuis.html>pakhuis</a></span></span></dd></dl></li>
<li>A greenhouse in which crop rotation <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> practised.</li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:warenhuis.html>warenhuis</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic"><a href = vnd.unilang:o.html>o</a></span>

***warlock.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:warlock.html>warlock</a> (50298)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warloghe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warlowe</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">warloȝe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wǣrloga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">traitor, deceiver</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span>, literally <span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truce-breaker</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">wǣr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:convenant.html>covenant</a>, truce, pact, promise</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*weh₁-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">true</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>; whence also <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">vērus</i>) + <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">loga</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">liar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*lugô</i>, related to Old English <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">lēogan</i> (whence English <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">lie</i>). The hard <i>-ck</i> ending originated in Scottish and Northern English, like the sense "male magic-user" (from the notion that such <a href = vnd.unilang:men.html>men</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:were.html>were</a> in league with the Devil). Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">wārlogo</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">truce-breaker, traitor</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p><p>A few writers alternatively propose derivation from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">varðlokkur</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">caller of <a href = vnd.unilang:spirits.html>spirits</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>,<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> but as the <i>OED</i> notes, this <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> implausible due to the extreme rarity of the <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a> word and because forms without hard <i>-k</i>, which are consistent with the Old English etymology (“traitor”), are attested earlier than forms with <i>-k</i>,<sup id="cite_ref-2" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-2"> | 2 | </a></sup> and forms with <i>-ð-</i> are not attested.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:warlock.html>warlock</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">warlocks</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A male magic-user; a male witch.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li>Because of its etymology, the term <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not used by some male witches, who prefer other <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a> like <i>witch</i> instead.<sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-4" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-4"> | 4 | </a></sup><sup id="cite_ref-5" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-5"> | 5 | </a></sup></li></ul>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*warmaz</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*gʷʰer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:warm.html>warm</a>, hot</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> or alternatively <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wer-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to burn</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***warrig.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:warrig.html>warrig</a> (39962)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">war</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ig</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adjective">Adjective</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warrig.html>warrig</a></strong> (<i>comparative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:warrig.html>warriger</a></b>, <i>superlative</i> <b class="Latn" lang="nl">warrigst</b>)
</p>

***wasbeer.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wasbeer.html>wasbeer</a> (17419)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wassen.html>wassen</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to wash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">bear</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Probably a loan translation of earlier  <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de">Waschbär</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wasbeer.html>wasbeer</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wasberen.html>wasberen</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wasbeertje.html>wasbeertje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>A raccoon, carnivore of the genus <i>Procyon</i>.
<ul><li><b>2008</b> July 9, "<a href = vnd.unilang:wasbeer.html>Wasbeer</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:trekt.html>trekt</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:verwoestend.html>verwoestend</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:spoor.html>spoor</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:door.html>door</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:belgische.html>Belgische</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bossen.html>bossen</a>", <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:laatste.html>Laatste</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nieuws.html>Nieuws</a></i>.
<dl><dd><a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>De</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wasberen.html>wasberen</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:leven.html>leven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:vooral.html>vooral</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:de.html>de</a> Ardennen.
<dl><dd>The <b>raccoons</b> predominantly live in the Ardennes.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">hespan</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="nl">muskuskat</span> <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">obsolete</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span></li>

***wassen.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wassen.html>wassen</a> (2154)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">wasschen</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wascan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*waskaną</i>, ultimately from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*wed-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water, <a href = vnd.unilang:wet.html>wet</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wassen.html>wassen</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">transitive</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to wash, to clean</li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wassen.html>wassen</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">wassan</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*wahsijaną</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to increase</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*h₂weg-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to increase</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***wasteland.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a> (97127)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">waste</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>land</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">wastelands</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A region with no remaining resources; a desert.
<ul><li><b>2007</b>, Kai Hansen, "To Mother Earth", Gamma <a href = vnd.unilang:ray.html>Ray</a>, <i><a href = vnd.unilang:land.html>Land</a> of the Free II</i>.
<dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Here create another <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a></b> / On and on '<a href = vnd.unilang:til.html>til</a> nothing's there / Here it <a href = vnd.unilang:comes.html>comes</a>, the devastation / Poisoning the air</span></div></dd></dl></li></ul>
<dl><dd><i>Ten years of drought <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> left the area a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a></b>.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li>Any barren or uninteresting place.
<dl><dd><i>After his experiences, he no longer found western Kansas such a <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a></b>.</i></dd></dl>
<ul><li><b>1961</b> May 9, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Newton_N._Minow" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Newton N. Minow">Newton N. Minow</a>, "<a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Television_and_the_Public_Interest" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Television and the Public Interest">Television and the Public Interest</a>":
<dl><dd>Keep your <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a> glued to that set until the station <a href = vnd.unilang:signs.html>signs</a> off. I can assure you that what you will observe <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a <a href = vnd.unilang:vast.html>vast</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wasteland.html>wasteland</a></b>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
</body>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*hwat</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Indo-European_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Indo-European language">Proto-Indo-European</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷód</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ine-pro">*kʷod</i>, compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/West_Frisian_language" class="extiw" title="w:West Frisian language">West Frisian</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fy"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">what</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a></i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">hvad</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Pronoun_3">Pronoun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">interrogative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what: e.g. (1) asking for a subject complement; (2) asking for a sentence object
<dl><dd>(1) <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a>?</i>  |  <i>What</i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> that?</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>Wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:je.html>je</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>?</i>  |  <i>What</i> do you want to do?</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> what: e.g. (1) as the object of a sentence; (2) ditto
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:weet.html>weet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:niet.html>niet</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doen.html>doen</a>.</i>  |  I don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> know <i>what</i> I want to do.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>Jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moet.html>moet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:afblijven.html>afblijven</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:van.html>van</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:jij.html>jij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ziet.html>ziet</a>.</i>  |  You must not touch <i>what</i> you see there.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> that: e.g. (1) modifying an indefinite pronoun like <a href = vnd.unilang:iets.html>iets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:niets.html>niets</a>, <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:enige.html>enige</a>; (2) modifying an adjective that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> used as a noun, usually a superlative
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:geef.html>Geef</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:mij.html>mij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:maar.html>maar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:alles.html>alles</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:eetbaar.html>eetbaar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a>.</i>  |  Please give <a href = vnd.unilang:me.html>me</a> everything that <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> edible.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>Het</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:duurste.html>duurste</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:er.html>er</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</i>  |  The most expensive <i>that</i> there <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">relative</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> which: e.g. (1) modifying the demonstrative pronouns <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> and datgene; (2) referring back to an entire sentence
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:nam.html>nam</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:precies.html>precies</a> datgene <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:gewild.html>gewild</a></i>  |  He <a href = vnd.unilang:took.html>took</a> exactly that <i>which</i> I <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wanted.html>wanted</a>.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:jantje.html>Jantje</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:deed.html>deed</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:het.html>het</a> in z’n <a href = vnd.unilang:broek.html>broek</a>, <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:zijn.html>zijn</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:moeder.html>moeder</a> in <a href = vnd.unilang:verlegenheid.html>verlegenheid</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:bracht.html>bracht</a>.</i>  |  John <a href = vnd.unilang:did.html>did</a> it in his <a href = vnd.unilang:pants.html>pants</a>, <i>which</i> embarrassed his mother</dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">indefinite</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> something: e.g. (1) as subject; (2) as subject complement
<dl><dd>(1) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:daar.html>Daar</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:loopt.html>loopt</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:rond.html>rond</a>.</i>  |  <i>Something</i> there <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> walking around.</dd>
<dd>(2) <i><a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>Dat</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:aardig.html>aardig</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b>!</i>  |  That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> quite <i>something</i>! [i.e. "That <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> quite a lot!"]</dd></dl></li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Usage_notes">Usage notes</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p>This pronoun can combine with a preposition to form a pronominal adverb. When this occurs, it <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> changed into its adverbial/locative counterpart <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:waar.html>waar</a></i>. See also Category:Dutch pronominal adverbs.
</p><p>A subclause following the relative pronoun <i><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></i> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> in SOV order.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Determiner_2">Determiner</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>some
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:ik.html>Ik</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:wil.html>wil</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:graag.html>graag</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:kersen.html>kersen</a>.</i>
<dl><dd>I want <b>some</b> cherries please.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Adverb_3">Adverb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li>a bit, somewhat
<dl><dd><i><a href = vnd.unilang:hij.html>Hij</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:doet.html>doet</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:dat.html>dat</a> <b><a href = vnd.unilang:wat.html>wat</a></b> onbedachtzaam.</i>
<dl><dd>He does that <b>somewhat</b> unthoughtfully.</dd></dl></dd></dl></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:wateren.html>wateren</a></i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">weteren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*wateron</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">*weteren</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*watrōną</i>, <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*watrijaną</i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">water</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-en</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>

<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> common euphemism</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to urinate</li></ol>

<li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">irrigate</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:begieten.html>begieten</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:weken.html>weken</a></span></li></ul>

<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">water</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">water</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:pas.html>pas</a></i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">fit, measure</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.
